- [Brick 12 In. X 12 In. Vinyl Peel and Stick Backsplash Tiles in Black Grey (10-Sheets)](https://smartspaceguide.com/products/brick-12-in-x-12-in-vinyl-peel-and-stick-backsplash-tiles-in-black-grey-10-sheets): Features 10 sheets of self-adhesive 3D tiles for walls Designed to be flexible and humidity resistant Perfect tiles to sustain kitchen and bathroom backsplashes Art3dwallpenels peel and stick tiles are smart and unique products that will simplify your life. The tiles can be easily installed directly over existing panels or smooth surfaces. Especially designed for kitchen backsplashes and bathroom backsplashes, the tiles are resistant to the heat of stovetops and the humidity of bathrooms. Installation Surface requirement: the tile needs to be installed over a clean and sleek surface. Please note that rough surfaces such as porous wood, embossed ceramic tiles, or textured wallpaper are not suitable to install. Not all the latex/repainted walls can be installed directly, for latex or repainted wall, we recommend using the 3M Spray Adhesive to give the installation extra protection. Tiles should not direct contact with flames, steam, or submerge in water. Do not install tiles less than 16 in away from the top of the stove. The new arrived peel and stick wall tiles may have little gel smell. The smell will dispel in 2-days to 3-days. If you want to remove the tile, you could use a hairdryer to warm up the adhesive and pull softly, starting with the corners. Then use a cleaning product to remove the excess glue left in. x the peel and stick tiles.
